  Here are the details:
  
  Endpoint: GET https://api.scrapecreators.com/v1/tiktok/video/transcript
  
  Description: Scrapes transcript from a TikTok video
  
  Required Headers:
  - x-api-key: Your API key
  
  Parameters:
  - url  (Required): TikTok video URL
- language : Language of the transcript. 2 letter language code, ie 'en', 'es', 'fr', 'de', 'it', 'ja', 'ko', 'zh'
- use_ai_as_fallback : Set to 'true' to use AI as a fallback to get the transcript if the transcript is not found. Costs 10 credits to use this feature.

  I want to make an API call to https://api.scrapecreators.com/v1/instagram/user/reels. 

  Please help me write code to make this API call and handle the response appropriately. Include error handling and best practices.

  Here are the details:
  
  Endpoint: GET https://api.scrapecreators.com/v1/instagram/user/reels
  
  Description: Get all public reels from a profile. Can provide a user_id or handle, but for faster response times, use user_id. This won't include pinned reels right now. And I'm not sure why, but it looks like IG doesn't return the description of the reel on this endpoint :( You'll have to use the post detail endpoint to get that.
  
  Required Headers:
  - x-api-key: Your API key
  
  Parameters:
  - user_id : Instagram user id. Use this for faster response times.
- handle : Instagram handle. Use user_id for faster response times.
- max_id : Max id to get more reels. Get 'max_id' from previous response.
- trim : Set to true for a trimmed down version of the response
  
  Example Response:
  {
  "items": [
    {
      "media": {
        "taken_at": 1736294201,
        "pk": "3540614075954356349",
        "id": "3540614075954356349_2700692569",
